 (define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))

)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)

    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))

    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (connected ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (connected ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (closed ?loc1 ?dir))
    :effect (and (open ?loc1 ?dir) (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (connected ?from ?to ?dir) (open ?from ?dir))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)
